name:S‚Äçh‚Äçu‚Äçi‚Äçz‚Äçh‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçl‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçm‚Äçe‚Äçi

posted:Posted June 4, 2024
msg:This is a hotel with surprises everywhere üòÑ I came here for the location and environment. The Eco-City is relatively close to the National Maritime Museum and the seaside of the Dongdi Park in the Mazu Cultural Park. There are special snack shops and traditional Tianjin restaurants around the hotel, as well as a small animation park to visit. The hotel itself has an even better environment, with a garden-style style and is pet-friendly. There are also various small animals that can be directly touched. It is packed on weekends, with many children and families staying, some taking their dogs for a walk, some children feeding alpacas and deer, and some families going swimming. The atmosphere is particularly comfortable, making people relax unconsciously. It is very suitable for vacation. What's more surprising is that the hotel service is worthy of the five-star high-end quality. The service ambassador Wu Tong was caring and thoughtful throughout the whole process. He called two days before check-in to understand our special needs. After knowing that the child has asthma, he arranged to upgrade to a high-end king-size bed non-smoking room and placed an air purifier in advance. After check-in, he gave fruit coupons and carefully asked if there were any other needs. He also introduced the surrounding tours attentively. The Chinese restaurant on the second floor has authentic Tianjin cuisine and Cantonese cuisine. I didn't want to go out for dinner and I was very satisfied with the food there. I really didn't want to leave after staying for three days. My son said that he would invite his friends to stay together again during the summer vacation.
The small flaw that does not cover the merits is that objectively speaking, the decoration of the house is a bit old. Although it is very clean and the bedding is comfortable to sleep on, the carpet will have a bit of old smell, but compared to enjoying a good living experience, these small problems can be ignored. I look forward to staying in Hilton again when I come to Binhai next time.

When I returned to the hotel, I found that the refrigerator had been replaced and the balcony seal could be opened. Full marks for response speed!
It was time for check-in to coincide with the birthday of the elderly family member. The hotel sent a birthday cake with a birthday hat and candles. It was really not the kind of small dessert-like cake sent by other hotels, which also surprised us.

The bowls of yogurt are particularly delicious. The staff collected the dishes promptly. There will be a wait for a table during peak periods, but it won't be long.
